Code to be Reviewed: routes/tickets.py\n```Code\n## routes/tickets.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import List\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.tickets import TicketCreate, TicketUpdate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/report", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/{ticket_id}/status", response_model=bool)\ndef update_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, status_update: TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: models.MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    return new_message\n\n```\n\n\n\n# Format example 1\n## Code Review: routes/tickets.py\n1. """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef import Column, Integer, String, ForeignKey, DateTime\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import relationship\nimport datetime\n\nBase = declarative_base()\n\nclass User(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'users\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    username = Column(String, unique=True, nullable=False)\n    password_hash = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    \n    tickets = relationship("Ticket", back_populates="user")\n    messages = relationship("Message", back_populates="ticket")\n\n    def __init__(self, username: str, password_hash: str):\n        self.username = username\n        self.password_hash = password_hash\n\n    def login(self) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual authentication logic\n        return True  # Assume successful login for now\n\n    def report_ticket(self, title: str, description: str) -> \'Ticket\':\n        ticket = Ticket(title=title, description=description)\n        ticket.user_id = self.id\n        return ticket\n\n    def modify_ticket(self, ticket_id: int, status: str) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual logic to update ticket status\n        return True  # Assume successful modification for now\n\n\nclass Ticket(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'tickets\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\'users.id\'), nullable=False)\n    title = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    description = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    status = Column(String, default=\'new\', nullable=False)\n\n    user = relationship("User", back_populates="tickets")\n\n    def __init__(self, title: str, description: str):\n        self.title = title\n        self.description = description\n\n    def update_status(self, status: str) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual logic to update ticket status\n        self.status = status\n        return True  # Assume successful update for now\n\n\nclass Message(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'messages\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    ticket_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\'tickets.id\'), nullable=False)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\'users.id\'), nullable=False)\n    content = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)\n\n    ticket = relationship("Ticket", back_populates="messages")\n\n    def __init__(self, content: str):\n        self.content = content\n\n    def send_message(self, ticket_id: int, content: str) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual logic to send message\n        return True  # Assume successful message sending for now\n\n\nclass Database(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'database\'\n    \n    engine = None\n    SessionLocal = None\n    \n    @classmethod\n    def create_tables(cls):\n        cls.engine = Base.metadata.create_all(bind=cls.engine)\n        \n    @classmethod\n    def get_db(cls) -> Generator[Session, None, None]:\n        db: Optional[Session] = None\n        try:\n            db = cls.SessionLocal()\n            yield db\n        finally:\n            if db:\n                db.close()\n```\n----- routes/tickets.py\n```## routes/tickets.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import List\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.tickets import TicketCreate, TicketUpdate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/report", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/{ticket_id}/status", response_model=bool)\ndef update_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, status_update: TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: models.MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    return new_message\n```\n```\n\n## Debug logs\n```text\n\n\n\n```\n\n## Bug Feedback logs\n```text\n\n```\n\n# Format example\n## Code: routes/users.py\n```python\n## routes/users.py\n...\n```\n\n# routes/tickets.py\n```## routes/tickets.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import List\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.tickets import TicketCreate, TicketUpdate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/report", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/{ticket_id}/status", response_model=bool)\ndef update_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, status_update: TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: models.MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    return new_message\n```\n\n\n## Code to be Reviewed: routes/users.py\n```Code\n## routes/users.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom  :param user_data: UserLogin object containing username and password\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the login was successful\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, user_data.username)\n    if not user or not user.login():\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid credentials")\n    \n    return True\n\n@router.post("/report_ticket", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: models.TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate object containing title and description\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/modify_ticket/{ticket_id}", response_model=bool)\ndef modify_ticket(ticket_id: int, status_update: models.TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the update was successful\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.put("/modify_user/{user_id}", response_model=bool)\ndef modify_user(user_data: UserCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Modify user details.\n    \n    :param user_data: UserCreate object containing updated username and password\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the update was successful\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_id(db, user_data.id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    user.username = user_data.username\n    user.password_hash = user_data.password_hash\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n```\n\n\n\n# Format example 1\n## Code routes/tickets.py\n```## routes/tickets.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import List\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.tickets import TicketCreate, TicketUpdate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/report", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/{ticket_id}/status", response_model=bool)\ndef update_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, status_update: TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: models.MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    return new_message\n```\n\n\n## Code to be Reviewed: routes/users.py\n```Code\n## routes/users.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom new_message\n```\n----- routes/users.py\n```## routes/users.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import Optional\nimport API"}\n\n# Dependency to get the database session\ndef get_db_session() -> Session:\n    db: Optional[Session] = None\n    try:\n        db = next(get_db())\n        yield db\n    finally:\n        if import Column, Integer, String, ForeignKey, DateTime\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import relationship\nimport datetime\n\nBase = declarative_base()\n\nclass User(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'users\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    username = Column(String, unique=True, nullable=False)\n    password_hash = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    \n    tickets = relationship("Ticket", back_populates="user")\n    messages = relationship("Message", back_populates="ticket")\n\n    def __init__(self, username: str, password_hash: str):\n        self.username = username\n        self.password_hash = password_hash\n\n    def login(self) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual authentication logic\n        return True  # Assume successful login for now\n\n    def report_ticket(self, title: str, description: str) -> \'Ticket\':\n        ticket = Ticket(title=title, description=description)\n        ticket.user_id = self.id\n        return ticket\n\n    def modify_ticket(self, ticket_id: int, status: str) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual logic to update ticket status\n        return True  # Assume successful modification for now\n\n\nclass Ticket(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'tickets\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\'users.id\'), nullable=False)\n    title = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    description = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    status = Column(String, default=\'new\', nullable=False)\n\n    user = relationship("User", back_populates="tickets")\n\n    def __init__(self, title: str, description: str):\n        self.title = title\n        self.description = description\n\n    def update_status(self, status: str) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual logic to update ticket status\n        self.status = status\n        return True  # Assume successful update for now\n\n\nclass Message(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'messages\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    ticket_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\'tickets.id\'), nullable=False)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\'users.id\'), nullable=False)\n    content = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.datetime.utcnow)\n\n    ticket = relationship("Ticket", back_populates="messages")\n\n    def __init__(self, content: str):\n        self.content = content\n\n    def send_message(self, ticket_id: int, content: str) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual logic to send message\n        return True  # Assume successful message sending for now\n\n\nclass Database(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'database\'\n    \n    engine = None\n    SessionLocal = None\n    \n    @classmethod\n    def create_tables(cls):\n        cls.engine = Base.metadata.create_all(bind=cls.engine)\n        \n    @classmethod\n    def get_db(cls) -> Generator[Session, None, None]:\n        db: Optional[Session] = None\n        try:\n            db = cls.SessionLocal()\n            yield db\n        finally:\n            if db:\n                db.close()\n```\n----- routes/tickets.py\n```## routes/tickets.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import List\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.tickets import TicketCreate, TicketUpdate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/report", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/{ticket_id}/status", response_model=bool)\ndef update_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, status_update: TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: models.MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    return new_message\n```\n----- routes/users.py\n```## routes/users.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import Optional\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.users import UserCreate, UserLogin\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/login", response_model=bool)\ndef login(user_data: UserLogin, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    User login.\n    \n    :param user_data: UserLogin object containing username and password\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the login was successful\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, user_data.username)\n    if not user or not user.login():\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid credentials")\n    \n    return True\n\n@router.post("/report_ticket", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: models.TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate object containing title and description\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/modify_ticket/{ticket_id}", response_model=bool)\ndef modify_ticket(ticket_id: int, status_update: models.TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the update was successful\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.put("/modify_user/{user_id}", response_model=bool)\ndef modify_user(user_data: UserCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Modify user details.\n    \n    :param user_data: UserCreate object containing updated username and password\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the update was successful\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_id(db, user_data.id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    user.username = user_data.username\n    user.password_hash = user_data.password_hash\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n```\n----- routes/messages.py\n```## routes/messages.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import Optional\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.messages import MessageCreate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    # Get the ticket by its ID\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    \n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    # Create a new message with the provided content and associate it with the ticket\n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    \n    # Add the new message to the database session and commit the changes\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    \n    return new_message\n```\n```\n\n## Debug logs\n```text\n\n\n\n```\n\n## Bug Feedback logs\n```text\n\n```\n\n# Format example\n## Code: db:\n            db.close()\n\n@app.on_event("shutdown")\ndef shutdown_event():\n    # Ensure all resources are closed on shutdown\n    pass\n\n# Example of a simple health check endpoint\n@app.get("/health")\ndef health_check():\n    return {"status": "ok"}\n```\n----- models.py\n```## models.py\n\nfrom sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base\nfrom sqlalchemy import Column, Integer, String, ForeignKey, DateTime\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import relationship\nimport datetime\n\nBase = declarative_base()\n\nclass User(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'users\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    username = Column(String, unique=True, nullable=False)\n    password_hash = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    \n    tickets =   def report_ticket(self, title: str, description: str) -> \'Ticket\':\n        ticket = Ticket(title=title, description=description)\n        ticket.user_id = self.id\n        return ticket\n\n Column(String, nullable=False)\n    description = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    status = Column(String, default=\'new\', nullable=False)\n\n    user = relationship("User", back_populates="tickets")\n\n    def __init__(self, title: str, description: str):\n        self.title = title\n        self.description = description\n\n    def update_status(self, status: str) -> bool:\n        # Placeholder for actual logic to update ticket status\n        self.status = status\n        return True  # Assume successful update for now\n\n\nclass Message(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \'messages\'\n    \n    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, index=True)\n    ticket_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey(\'tickets.id\'), nullable=False)\n    user_id = Column(Integer, None\n    \n    @classmethod\n    def create_tables(cls):\n        cls.engine = Base.metadata.create_all(bind=cls.engine)\n        \n    @classmethod\n    def get_db(cls) -> Generator[Session, None, None]:\n        db: Optional[Session] = None\n        try:\n            db = cls.SessionLocal()\n            yield db\n        finally:\n            if db:\n                db.close()\n```\n----- routes/tickets.py\n```## routes/tickets.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import List\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.tickets import TicketCreate, TicketUpdate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/report", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/{ticket_id}/status", response_model=bool)\ndef update_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, status_update: TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: models.MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    return new_message\n```\n----- routes/users.py\n```## routes/users.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import Optional\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.users import UserCreate, UserLogin\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/login", response_model=bool)\ndef login(user_data: UserLogin, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    User login.\n    \n    :param user_data: UserLogin object containing username and password\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the login was successful\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, user_data.username)\n    if not user or not user.login():\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid credentials")\n    \n    return True\n\n@router.post("/report_ticket", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: models.TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate object containing title and description\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return new_ticket\n\n@router.put("/modify_ticket/{ticket_id}", response_model=bool)\ndef modify_ticket(ticket_id: int, status_update: models.TicketUpdate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Update the status of a ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param status_update: TicketUpdate object containing new status\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the update was successful\n    """\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.put("/modify_user/{user_id}", response_model=bool)\ndef modify_user(user_data: UserCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Modify user details.\n    \n    :param user_data: UserCreate object containing updated username and password\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Success flag indicating if the update was successful\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_id(db, user_data.id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    user.username = user_data.username\n    user.password_hash = user_data.password_hash\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n```\n----- routes/messages.py\n```## routes/messages.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import Optional\nimport models  # Assuming models are defined in the models.py file\nfrom database import get_db  # Importing session creation function from database module\nfrom schemas.messages import MessageCreate\n\nrouter = APIRouter()\n\n@router.post("/{ticket_id}/messages", response_model=models.Message, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef send_message(ticket_id: int, message_data: MessageCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Send a message for the ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_id: ID of the ticket\n    :param message_data: MessageCreate object containing message content\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created message\n    """\n    # Get the ticket by its ID\n    ticket = models.Ticket.get_ticket_by_id(db, ticket_id)\n    \n    if not ticket:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Ticket not found")\n    \n    # Create a new message with the provided content and associate it with the ticket\n    new_message = models.Message(content=message_data.content)\n    new_message.ticket_id = ticket.id\n    \n    # Add the new message to the database session and commit the changes\n    db.add(new_message)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_message)\n    \n    return new_message\n```\n```\n\n## Debug logs\n```text\n\n\n\n```\n\n## Bug Feedback logs\n```text\n\n```\n\n# Format example\n## Code: True\n\n@router.post("/report_ticket", response_model=models.Ticket, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\ndef report_ticket(ticket_data: models.TicketCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):\n    """\n    Report a new ticket.\n    \n    :param ticket_data: TicketCreate object containing title and description\n    :param db: Database session\n    :return: Created ticket\n    """\n    user = models.User.get_user_by_username(db, ticket_data.user_id)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    \n    new_ticket = models.Ticket(title=ticket_data.title, description=ticket_data.description)\n    new_ticket.user_id = user.id\n    db.add(new_ticket)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(new_ticket)\n    return found")\n    \n    ticket.update_status(status_update.status)\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n\n@router.put("/modify_user/{user_id}", response_model=bool)\ndef modify_user(user_data: UserCreate, detail="User not found")\n    \n    user.username = user_data.username\n    user.password_hash = user_data.password_hash\n    db.commit()\n    return True\n```\n----- routes/messages.py\n```## routes/tickets.py\n```## routes/tickets.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom typing import List\nimport models  # Assuming declarative_base\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker\n\nBase = declarative_base()\n\nclass Database:\n    def __init__(self, engine_url: str):\n        """\n        Initialize the database with a given engine URL.\n        \n        :param engine_url: The connection string for the database engine.\n        """\n        self.engine = sa.create_engine(engine_url)\n        Base.metadata.bind = self.engine\n        SessionLocal = sessionmaker(autocommit=False, autoflush=False, bind=self.engine)\n        self.SessionLocal = SessionLocal\n\n    @classmethod\n    def create_tables(cls, engine_url: str):\n        """\n        Create all tables in the database.\n        \n        :param engine_url: The connection string for the database engine.\n        """\n        with cls(engine_url) as db:\n            Base.metadata.create_all(bind=db.engine)\n\n    @classmethod\n    def get_db(cls, engine_url: str) -> \'Generator[Session, None, None]\':\n        """\n        Get a database session generator.\n        \n        :param engine_url: The connection string for the database engine.\n        :return: A generator yielding a database session.\n        """\n        db = None\n        try:\n            with cls(engine_url) as db:\n                yield db\n        finally:\n            if db:\n                db.close()\n\n    def __enter__(self):\n        return self.SessionLocal()\n\n    def __exit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):\n        pass\n\n# Example usage of the Database class\nif __name__ == "__main__":\n    engine_url = "sqlite:///example.db"\n    db = Database(engine_url)\n    db.create_tables(engine_url)\n\n```\n\n\n\n# Format example 1\n## Code Review: database.py\n1. Reviewed: routes.py\n```Code\n## routes.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException\nfrom flask import request, jsonify\nimport datetime\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom models import User, Ticket, Message, HelpdeskStaff, DatabaseAPI, MicroservicesAPI  # Import data model definitions\nfrom microservices_api import MicroservicesAPI  # Import microservices API logic\n\n# Initialize router for FastAPI\nuser_router = APIRouter()\nticket_router = APIRouter()\n\n# Dependency injection for database session\ndef get_db_session() -> Session:\n    db_session = DatabaseAPI.create_db_session()  # Assume create_db_session is defined in models.py\n    try:\n        yield db_session\n    finally:\n        db_session.close()\n\n@user_router.post(\'/users/login\')\nasync def login(username: str, password_hash: str) -> dict:\n    user = MicroservicesAPI.get_user_by_username(db_api=Depends(get_db_session), username=username)\n    if not user or not bcrypt.checkpw(password_hash.encode(\'utf-8\'), user.password_hash.encode(\'utf-8\')):\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid credentials")\n    return {"message": "Login successful"}\n\n@ticket_router.post(\'/tickets/report-issue\')\nasync def report_issue(username: str, issue: str) -> dict:\n    db_session = get_db_session()\n    user = MicroservicesAPI.get_user_by_username(db_api=db_session, username=username)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    ticket = user.report_issue(issue=issue)\n    return {"ticket_id": ticket.id}\n\n@ticket_router.get(\'/tickets/view-tickets\')\nasync def view_tickets(status: str) -> list[dict]:\n    db_session = get_db_session()\n    tickets = MicroservicesAPI.view_tickets(db_api=db_session, status=status)\n    return [{"id": t.id, "user_id": t.user_id, "issue": t.issue, "status": t.status} for t in tickets]\n\n@ticket_router.put(\'/tickets/modify-ticket-status\')\nasync def modify_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, new_status: str) -> dict:\n    db_session = get_db_session()\n    success = MicroservicesAPI.change_ticket_status(db_api=db_session, ticket_id=ticket_id, new_status=new_status)\n    if not success:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Failed to update ticket status")\n    return {"message": "Ticket status updated successfully"}\n\n# Register routers for FastAPI\ndef register_fastapi_routers(fastapi_app: FastAPI):\n    fastapi_app.include_router(user_router, prefix="/users")\n    fastapi_app.include_router(ticket_router, prefix="/tickets")\n\n# Register routes for Flask application\ndef register_flask_routes(flask_app: Flask):\n    @flask_app.route(\'/users/login\', methods=[\'POST\'])\n    def login_route():\n        data = request.get_json()\n        username = data.get(\'username\')\n        password_hash = data.get(\'password_hash\')\n        return jsonify(login(username, password_hash))\n\n    @flask_app.route(\'/tickets/report-issue\', methods=[\'POST\'])\n    def report_issue_route():\n        data = request.get_json()\n        username = data.get(\'username\')\n        issue = data.get(\'issue\')\n        return jsonify(report_issue(username, issue))\n\n    @flask_app.route(\'/tickets/view-tickets\', methods=[\'GET\'])\n    def view_tickets_route():\n        status = request.args.get(\'status\')\n        return jsonify(view_tickets(status=status))\n\n    @flask_app.route(\'/tickets/modify-ticket-status\', methods=[\'PUT\'])\n    def modify_ticket_status_route():\n        data = request.get_json()\n        ticket_id = data.get(\'ticket_id\')\n        new_status = data.get(\'new_status\')\n        return jsonify(modify_ticket_status(ticket_id=ticket_id, new_status=new_status))\n\n```\n\n\n\n# Format routes.py\n```## routes.py\n\nfrom fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException\nfrom flask import request, jsonify\nimport datetime\nfrom sqlalchemy.orm import Session\nfrom models import User, Ticket, Message, HelpdeskStaff, DatabaseAPI, MicroservicesAPI  # Import data model definitions\nfrom microservices_api import MicroservicesAPI  # Import microservices API logic\n\n# Initialize router for FastAPI\nuser_router = APIRouter()\nticket_router = APIRouter()\n\n# Dependency injection for database session\ndef get_db_session() -> Session:\n    db_session = DatabaseAPI.create_db_session()  # Assume create_db_session is defined in models.py\n    try:\n        yield db_session\n    finally:\n        db_session.close()\n\n@user_router.post(\'/users/login\')\nasync def login(username: str, password_hash: str) -> dict:\n    user = MicroservicesAPI.get_user_by_username(db_api=Depends(get_db_session), username=username)\n    if not user or not bcrypt.checkpw(password_hash.encode(\'utf-8\'), user.password_hash.encode(\'utf-8\')):\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Invalid credentials")\n    return {"message": "Login successful"}\n\n@ticket_router.post(\'/tickets/report-issue\')\nasync def report_issue(username: str, issue: str) -> dict:\n    db_session = get_db_session()\n    user = MicroservicesAPI.get_user_by_username(db_api=db_session, username=username)\n    if not user:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="User not found")\n    ticket = user.report_issue(issue=issue)\n    return {"ticket_id": ticket.id}\n\n@ticket_router.get(\'/tickets/view-tickets\')\nasync def view_tickets(status: str) -> list[dict]:\n    db_session = get_db_session()\n    tickets = MicroservicesAPI.view_tickets(db_api=db_session, status=status)\n    return [{"id": t.id, "user_id": t.user_id, "issue": t.issue, "status": t.status} for t in tickets]\n\n@ticket_router.put(\'/tickets/modify-ticket-status\')\nasync def modify_ticket_status(ticket_id: int, new_status: str) -> dict:\n    db_session = get_db_session()\n    success = MicroservicesAPI.change_ticket_status(db_api=db_session, ticket_id=ticket_id, new_status=new_status)\n    if not success:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Failed to update ticket status")\n    return {"message": "Ticket status updated successfully"}\n\n# Register routers for FastAPI\ndef register_fastapi_routers(fastapi_app: FastAPI):\n    fastapi_app.include_router(user_router, prefix="/users")\n    fastapi_app.include_router(ticket_router, prefix="/tickets")\n\n# Register routes for Flask application\ndef register_flask_routes(flask_app: Flask):\n    @flask_app.route(\'/users/login\', methods=[\'POST\'])\n    def login_route():\n        data = request.get_json()\n        username = data.get(\'username\')\n        password_hash = data.get(\'password_hash\')\n        return jsonify(login(username, password_hash))\n\n    @flask_app.route(\'/tickets/report-issue\', methods=[\'POST\'])\n    def report_issue_route():\n        data = request.get_json()\n        username = data.get(\'username\')\n        issue = data.get(\'issue\')\n        return jsonify(report_issue(username, issue))\n\n    @flask_app.route(\'/tickets/view-tickets\', methods=[\'GET\'])\n    def view_tickets_route():\n        status = request.args.get(\'status\')\n        return jsonify(view_tickets(status=status))\n\n    @flask_app.route(\'/tickets/modify-ticket-status\', methods=[\'PUT\'])\n    def modify_ticket_status_route():\n        data = request.get_json()\n        ticket_id = data.get(\'ticket_id\')\n        new_status = data.get(\'new_status\')\n        return jsonify(modify_ticket_status(ticket_id=ticket_id, new_status=new_status))\n```\n```\n\n## Debug
